Third, the little brother who checked in at the front desk helped me move to the executive floor on the 21st floor. However, due to the south, the highest daytime temperature on April 28 was 28 degrees, and the room was 26.3 degrees. The temperature dropped in the next two days, and I felt much more comfortable. Power-saving awareness is commendable, but it should not be more humane. It is strongly recommended to close the curtains in rooms 02 to 08 during the day to avoid direct sunlight. Consider a shaded room. The fourth is that I booked a double breakfast on Ctrip. Because I want to take my children on a trip, I added a breakfast with Ctrip points on the first day. I learned at the front desk that I could buy a breakfast for 88 yuan in the WeChat mall on the second or third day. I immediately bought two breakfasts. share. But when it was time to eat breakfast, the waiter told the room that there were three breakfast coupons, and then the account manager told the front desk that three breakfasts were needed, but the breakfast coupons bought in the mall could not be refunded! Unless it does it again this year, it's a loss. I hope the hotel will clarify the discounts that can be given in advance.
All in all, this hotel still deserves a cautious recommendation.

The executive lounge recommends replacing the coffee machine. It has been running out of water, and the water tank of the small coffee machine is too small.

There is a saying that the chrysanthemum rice noodles for breakfast are still very good, and a bowl of soup rice noodles starts the day full of vitality.

I feel that most of the gym and swimming pool of the Crowne Plaza are outsourced. There is nothing in itself. After all, the hotel needs to be profitable, but it is recommended to control the number of visitors, otherwise it will not feel very good for the guests.

msg:It is a five-star hotel highly recommended by Wuxi. It is located in the north of Taihu Square, west of the Grand Canal, 1.5 kilometers east of the Qingming Bridge, Nanchang Street, and Wuxi Museum and Science and Technology Museum across Taihu Square in the south. The hotel breakfast is very rich, the executive lounge and the Starbucks coffee on the first floor are very nice. The front desk service is fast and check out is fast. The Romanian lollipops and Yangshan water peaches promoted are very good. The room is very large, well-equipped, sanitary and clean, air conditioning is adjusted quickly, hot water is sufficient, and the bathtub is just a few minutes away. Very satisfied stay!
